# ttnn.to_layout

| Name | Input Shapes | Input Layouts | Attributes | Output Shapes | Output Layouts | Runs on TTNN | PCC | ATOL |
| ---- | ------------ | ------------- | ---------- | ------------- | -------------- | ------------ | --- | ---- |
| ttnn.to_layout | tensor<[32,1,1,f32]> | mapping_from: (d0, d1, d2), mapping_to: (d0 + d1, d2), memory_config: (32, 1, 'f32', 'system_memory') | layout: #ttnn.layout<tile> | tensor<[32,1,1,f32]> | mapping_from: (d0, d1, d2), mapping_to: (d0 + d1, d2), memory_config: (1, 1, 'tile<32x32, f32>', 'dram') | nan | nan |
